It's a very intuitive platform and you get handy all information needed to succeed. Once you are in, you start providing all the information about your website, but you can add as many websites as you want on the same account. Also, they recently added the choice to be paid through Payoneer which makes it very useful for many freelancers or bloggers.</p><p class="formatted-text"></p><p class="formatted-text">Awin is a platform that has been made for affiliate marketers, is a good option as long as your desirable company uses it in order to look for partnerships. But, remember that every platform is different and the rate for earning may be different too. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Awin?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">You have to pay a 5$ fee to get into the platform and you will get the fee back once you cash out but It can take a while to make it. </p><p class="formatted-text"></p><p class="formatted-text">Another thing I have to say is that the customer service isn't great. It can take a long time in order that someone can answer your questions so, I would suggest looking first at the answers on the faqs or in related blogs that talk about the common issues it may appear. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4831674 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering Awin:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Remember, it can take some time to achieve goals in affiliate marketing but Awin is just another platform that you can take into consideration as long as you can be patient and have a strategy behind it. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4831674 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Awin solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Awin has allowed me to be upfront with many possible companies looking for partnerships. Awin let me see my stats, clicks, converting rates of all the people that come to my website. </p><p class="formatted-text"></p><p class="formatted-text">If you are interested in Awin check first if the company you would like to work with is in there or at least check out which companies are useful for your blog or business at Awin before getting in. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized" ue="toggle-class login-modal-toggle" They may not have updated their review text, but have updated their review." aria-labelledby="icon-label-9ac64f4499439fb07b8f802a1b9aa2d2" role="img"><title id="icon-label-9ac64f4499439fb07b8f802a1b9aa2d2">Information</title><path d="M253 20c65 0 120 22 167 67 46 45 70 100 72 165 0 65-22 121-68 167-45 47-100 71-165 73-65 0-121-22-167-68-47-45-71-100-72-165S41 138 87 92c46-47 101-71 166-72m-1 379c10 0 19-3 25-9 6-7 10-15 10-24 0-11-2-19-9-26-6-6-15-9-25-9h-1c-10 0-18 3-24 9-7 6-10 14-11 24 0 10 3 18 10 25 6 6 14 10 24 10h1m85-168c9-11 13-24 13-40 0-26-9-46-27-59s-41-19-69-19c-22 0-40 4-53 13-24 14-36 39-37 75v2h56v-2c0-9 3-18 8-28 6-8 15-12 28-12 14 0 23 3 27 10 5 7 8 14 8 23 0 6-3 13-8 20-3 4-7 8-11 10l-3 2c-2 2-4 4-8 6-3 2-7 5-10 8-4 2-7 5-11 8s-7 6-9 9c-4 7-7 20-9 40v4h56v-2c0-4 0-9 2-14 2-7 6-13 14-19l14-9c16-12 25-20 29-26"></path></svg></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/awin-com/reviews/awin-review-4306937"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Great affiliate platform, especially for Etsy"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about Awin?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I like the Chrome extension which generates affiliate links quickly and easily across Awin advertisers. I use it specifically for Etsy products so it makes it so smooth to use it on-page. Also, the payment has always been timely, and I like that you can manage multiple vendors from your home screen. The comparative earnings analytics is helpful as well. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Awin?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I don't find their dashboard to be intuitive. I always have to figure it out again each time I log in, in order to get to my correct merchant and the earnings information I want.</p><p class="formatted-text"></p><p class="formatted-text">I find some of their participating affiliates obscure and have only found Etsy and 1-2 others that fit my offerings. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4306937 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering Awin:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I would use Awin if there's a significant affiliate partner that you want to work with. I wouldn't necessarily sign up just to see which companies you *could* work with. If there is someone like Etsy that is worth setting up an account, I think you'll find the payment smooth and the overall usability good. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4306937 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Awin solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I use it mainly to participate in the Etsy affiliate program, recommending specific products to my readers online. While it is not a huge portion of my income, it definitely enables me to monetize gift guides around the holiday season.</p><p class="formatted-text"></p><p class="formatted-text">I also have used it to browse their affiliate directory and brainstorm other affiliate partnerships. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex We previously used ImpactRadius, but the cost of ImpactRadius was higher than we liked. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about Awin?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The platform is easy to implement on a technical side. Tracking snippets are simple for any engineer to implement quickly.</p><p class="formatted-text">AWIN provides a decent API for additional data.</p><p class="formatted-text">Flexible rules for for different partners, allowing custom affiliate rates and groups. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4210407 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Awin?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">List of publishers that apply to our affiliate program are spam or low-rate publishers</p><p class="formatted-text">Finding partners or people to join your affiliate program is still on the affiliate program owner. The list of publishers are not great, and most don't provide value or are not in a similar market or country. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4210407 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering Awin:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">AWIN is good if you want a platform that can be the backend for your affiliate program, and will take care of tracking, reporting, and payments for you.</p><p class="formatted-text"></p><p class="formatted-text">AWIN will probably NOT help you find more people to join your affiliate program. They tout a large database of members, but most of those will not be successful  for your program (unless you want your coupon code everywhere...huge database of people with coupon websites) <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4210407 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Awin solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">AWIN provided the platform for our affiliate program used by our partners. AWIN makes it easy to have a hands-off affiliate program that takes care of billing, tracking, and reporting. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized x-login-modal-toggle-initialized" ue="toggle-class
